***разлепить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлепить.html>разлепи́ть</a> (23634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепить.html>лепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлепить.html>разлепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разлепля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unglue, to unstick</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to force apart, to open with difficulty (one's eyes, one's lips, etc.)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***разлетаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлетаться.html>разлета́ться</a> (12331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлетаться.html>разлета́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razletátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлететься.html>разлете́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly away, to scatter <i>(in the air)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлетаться.html>разлета́ются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мытье.html>мытья́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá vólosy <b>razletájutsja</b> pósle mytʹjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">my hair keeps flying away since I washed it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come apart, to be blown apart</li>
<li><i>(news, rumour etc)</i> to spread, to be spread about/around, to become known</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smash, to shatter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлетаться.html>разлета́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кусок.html>куски́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razletátʹsja</b> na kuskí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fly to bits; break into pieces/smithereens; smash to smithereens</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be ruined/shattered/squashed/upset</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полететь.html>полете́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poletétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">letátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:летающий.html>лета́ющий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">letájuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">лёт</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ljot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="переносное значение">перен.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="разговорное">разг.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:продаваться.html>продава́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:количество.html>коли́честве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>ма́лое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>Пла́тья</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлетаться.html>разлета́лись</a></span> — Лаура <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:открыть.html>откры́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>целую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сеть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:магазин.html>магази́нов</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

***разлететься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлететься.html>разлете́ться</a> (9331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>лете́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">letétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлететься.html>разлете́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razletétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлетаться.html>разлета́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fly away, to scatter <i>(in the air)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>листы́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлететься.html>разлете́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнате</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">listý <b>razletélisʹ</b> po kómnate</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the pages flew about the room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлететься.html>разлете́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>дым</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:разлететься.html>разлете́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прах.html>прах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razletétʹsja v dym; razletétʹsja v prax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go to pieces, fall to pieces, go to rack and ruin, go up in smoke</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come apart, to be blown apart</li>
<li><i>(news, rumour etc)</i> to spread, to be spread about/around, to become known
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новость.html>но́вость</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлететься.html>разлете́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́роду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nóvostʹ býstro <b>razletélasʹ</b> po górodu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the news was quickly spread around the town</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smash, to shatter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлететься.html>разлете́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кусок.html>куски́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razletétʹsja</b> na kuskí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fly to bits; break into pieces/smithereens; smash to smithereens</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be ruined/shattered/squashed/upset
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ши</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жды</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлететься.html>разлете́лись</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vse náši nadéždy <b>razletélisʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">all our hopes were dashed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***разлив.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́в</a> (16172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlív</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short past adverbial perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razlítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: having been poured</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlív</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлив.html>разли́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлив.html>разли́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлив.html>разли́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flood, overflow</li>
<li>bottling</li>

***разливать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разливать.html>разлива́ть</a> (8535)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razlítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разливать.html>разлива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spill</li>
<li>to pour out, to bottle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разливать.html>разлива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>чай</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razlivátʹ</b> čaj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pour the tea</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разливать.html>разлива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:суп.html>суп</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razlivátʹ</b> sup</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ladle out soup</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разливать.html>разлива́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вино́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razlivátʹ</b> vinó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pour the wine</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>водо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разольёшь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vodój ne <b>razolʹjóšʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">thick as thieves</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разливаться.html>разлива́ться</a> (13950)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разливать.html>разлива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razlivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разливаться.html>разлива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлиться.html>разли́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spill</li>
<li>to overflow</li>
<li>to spread</li>
<li>to pour out one's song</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разливать.html>разлива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razlivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***разлить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́ть</a> (8508)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разливать.html>разлива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spill</li>
<li>to pour out, to bottle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>водо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разольёшь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vodój ne razolʹjóšʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">thick as thieves</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разлиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлиться.html>разли́ться</a> (14551)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razlítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлиться.html>разли́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разливаться.html>разлива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spill
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> жёлчь <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлиться.html>разлила́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó žólčʹ <b>razlilásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has a bilious attack</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:румянец.html>румя́нец</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлиться.html>разлился</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rumjánec razlilsja po licú u kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">smb's face blushed/flushed; smb's cheeks glow</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to overflow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дожде́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>река́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлиться.html>разлила́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot doždéj reká <b>razlilásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the rains caused the river to overflow [to burst its banks]</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to spread</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлить.html>разли́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razlítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***различать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:различать.html>различа́ть</a> (4505)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:различить.html>различи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">različítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:различать.html>различа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">različátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:различить.html>различи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to distinguish, to tell apart, to tell the difference between two entities</li>
<li>to differ</li>
<li>to discriminate</li>
<li>to recognize</li></ol>

***различие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:различие.html>разли́чие</a> (5162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:различие.html>разли́чие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlíčije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:различие.html>разли́чия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:различие.html>разли́чия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:различие.html>разли́чий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>difference (quality of being different, used in a comparison)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:различие.html>разли́чие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́нах</a>  <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:европейский.html>европе́йских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́н</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razlíčije</b> v cénax  rússkix i jevropéjskix mašín</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the price difference between Russian and European cars</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разница.html>ра́зница</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ráznica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отличие.html>отли́чие</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otlíčije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">несхожесть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nesxožestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">непохожесть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nepoxožestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">несходство</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nesxodstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расхождение.html>расхожде́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rasxoždénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несоответствие.html>несоотве́тствие</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nesootvétstvije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">несовпаде́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nesovpadénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***различный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:различный.html>разли́чный</a> (1122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">líčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:различный.html>разли́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlíčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>different (not the same)</li>
<li>diverse, various</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разный.html>ра́зный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ráznyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разнообразный.html>разнообра́зный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raznoobráznyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́кий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vsjákij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***разложение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разложение.html>разложе́ние</a> (13024)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложение.html>разложе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razložénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложение.html>разложе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложение.html>разложе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложение.html>разложе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>decomposition, decay</li>
<li>dissolution, dissipation</li>
<li>corruption</li>
<li>dissociation</li>
<li>analysis <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">chemistry: process of breaking down a substance or the result of this process</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>putrefaction</li></ol>

***разложить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a> (5065)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раскладывать.html>раскла́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in separate locations</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to put away</li>
<li>to lay out, to display</li>
<li>to lay flat <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. a newspaper or cot</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to spread out (cards)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razložítʹ</b> kárty</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for a divination</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to spread the cards; <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for a game</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to deal the card</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to distribute, to apportion, to allocate</li>
<li>to build and light (a fire)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unharness</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагать.html>разлага́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to decompose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кислород.html>кислоро́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:водород.html>водоро́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razložítʹ</b> vódu na kisloród i vodoród</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to decompose/break water into oxygen and hydrogen</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to factorize
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>число́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> мно́жители</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razložítʹ</b> čisló na mnóžiteli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to factorize a number</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(force)</i> to resolve</li>
<li>to demoralize, to corrupt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:армия.html>а́рмию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razložítʹ</b> ármiju protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to demoralize/corrupt the enemy's army</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разложиться.html>разложи́ться</a> (26809)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложиться.html>разложи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razložítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагаться.html>разлага́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раскла́дываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to unpack
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раскла́дываться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raskládyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to unfold, to spread out, to open up, to open out
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раскла́дываться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raskládyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to decompose, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be factorized
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>число́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разложиться.html>разложи́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> мно́жители</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čisló <b>razložílosʹ</b> na mnóžiteli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the number was factorized</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагаться.html>разлага́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razlagátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to decompose, to rot, to decay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:труп.html>труп</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разложиться.html>разложи́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">trup <b>razložílsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the body decomposed</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагаться.html>разлага́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razlagátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get corrupted/demoralized
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:армия.html>а́рмия</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разложиться.html>разложи́лась</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ármija protívnika <b>razložílasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the enemy's army was demoralized</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлагаться.html>разлага́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razlagátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разложить.html>разложи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлом.html>разло́м</a> (29436)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлом.html>разло́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlóm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлом.html>разло́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлом.html>разло́мы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлом.html>разло́мов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>breaking, break-up</li>
<li>break</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fault, fracture, rupture</li></ol>

***разломать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разломать.html>разлома́ть</a> (24545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разломать.html>разлома́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlomátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разла́мывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break apart, to break into pieces
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разломить.html>разломи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razlomítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to destroy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломить.html>ломи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***разлука.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлука.html>разлу́ка</a> (7827)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлука.html>разлу́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razlúka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлука.html>разлу́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлука.html>разлу́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разлука.html>разлу́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>separation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлука.html>разлу́ке</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žitʹ v <b>razlúke</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">live apart; be separated</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>parting, separation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a> [<a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a>] <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разлука.html>разлу́ки</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čas [denʹ] <b>razlúki</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">hour [day] of parting</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
